### [257] [Personalizing Incremental Video Search with Hybrid Text and ID Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13493)
*Vivek Kanojiya,Vishalaksh Aggarwal,Daeho Baek,Lyndon Kennedy,Xuetao Yin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合文本语义嵌入（TextEmb）和ID协同嵌入（IdEmb）的Apple TV搜索个性化系统，通过XGBoost排序器融合用户历史行为信息。离线实验表明NDCG@10提升2.99%，MRR提升3.30%；在线实验显示点击率提升1.14%，转化率提升1.23%。尤其在模糊前缀查询（1-3字符）下，NDCG@10提升达8.63%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 增量式视频搜索中用户意图往往不明确（如仅输入1-3个字符前缀），传统非个性化排序无法为不同用户提供定制化结果。需要一种能在每个按键输入后实时提供高质量个性化排序的系统，尤其针对Apple TV这类智能电视搜索场景。

Method: 学习两个嵌入空间：1）基于文本的多语言编码器（TextEmb），通过对比学习在共参与三元组上微调；2）基于ID的协同过滤嵌入（IdEmb），在交互产生的正样本上训练。服务时，从用户近期观看历史构建用户表征，将文本和ID层面的用户-物品余弦相似度注入成对XGBoost排序器中。

Result: 离线：NDCG@10提升2.99%，MRR提升3.30%；模糊前缀查询（1-3字符）NDCG@10提升+8.63%（vs 完整查询+1.46%）；长历史用户（51-100项）NDCG提升+4.37%（vs 短历史+2.13%）。在线：点击率+1.14%，转化率+1.23%，转化物品排名提升2.91%。

Conclusion: 文本语义与协同过滤结合的方法在增量搜索个性化中效果显著，尤其对模糊查询和长历史用户价值最大。覆盖度与精度之间存在权衡，两种嵌入互为补充。通过LLM评判的相似度标签可减少点击/曝光偏差对嵌入质量评估的影响。

Abstract: Incremental video search requires high-quality ranking after each keystroke, where intent is often underspecified (e.g., 1-3 character prefixes). We present a personalization system for Apple TV search that combines complementary semantic and collaborative signals at ranking time. Our approach learns two item embedding spaces: (i) a text-based multilingual encoder (TextEmb) fine-tuned on co-engagement triplets via contrastive learning, and (ii) an ID-based collaborative embedding model (IdEmb) trained on interaction-derived positives. At serving time, we construct user representations from recent watch history and inject text- and ID-based user-item cosine similarities into a pairwise XGBoost ranker.
  We evaluate with temporally held-out offline datasets and a three-week online controlled experiment. Offline, for sessions with user history, the personalized ranker improves NDCG@10 by 2.99% and MRR by 3.30% over the non-personalized baseline. Slice analyses show that personalization is most needed in incremental search, where intent is still forming: on ambiguous prefix queries (1-3 characters), NDCG@10 lift is +8.63%, versus +1.46% on longer, fully specified queries. Longer-history users benefit more: NDCG lift rises from +2.13% for users with 1-5 history items to +4.37% for users with 51-100, even though baseline relevance is lower for these cohorts (NDCG@10 drops from 0.733 to 0.680), indicating that personalization adds the most value where default ranking underperforms. Online, treatment yields statistically significant gains of +1.14% tap-through rate and +1.23% conversion rate, with a 2.91% improvement in converted-item rank position. We further analyze coverage-precision trade-offs between semantic and collaborative embeddings via ablations isolating each signal, and evaluate embedding quality on a held-out corpus with LLM-judged similarity labels to reduce click/exposure bias.

</details>


### [258] [Cluster with Auctions for Vector Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13728)
*Swann Bessa,Pierre Fernandez,Gergely Szilvasy,Matthijs Douze,Hervé Jégou*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出CwA方法，通过联合学习平衡的数据库分区和神经探测函数，以优化近似最近邻搜索性能，在分布偏移场景下实现高达4.7倍吞吐量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统近似最近邻搜索中，查询探测函数与数据库分区常被绑定使用相同的分配函数，当查询分布与数据库分布不一致时性能严重下降。现有方法忽视了两者作为独立实体进行联合优化的必要性。

Method: CwA采用交替优化策略：(i) 对探测函数的神经网络进行梯度下降优化；(ii) 通过可并行化的拍卖算法进行大规模组合优化，实现数据库向量的平衡聚类分配。进一步引入笛卡尔积聚类扩展以提升分区粒度。

Result: 在分布偏移场景下，CwA相比最先进方法在同等召回率下实现最高4.7倍吞吐量；在分布内场景中，即使使用简单的线性探测函数也优于深度神经网络方法。

Conclusion: 将查询探测函数与数据库分区解耦并联合优化，能有效应对分布偏移问题，同时提升搜索效率与精度，为近似最近邻搜索提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Large-scale approximate nearest neighbor search commonly relies on partitions for indexing: database vectors are partitioned into clusters, and for each query a probing function selects the clusters to be scanned. The query probing function and the database partition are rarely treated as separate entities: most techniques assign queries with the same assignment function as the database vectors, which is suboptimal especially when database and query distributions differ. This paper introduces CwA (Cluster with Auctions), which addresses this limitation by jointly learning a balanced database partition and a neural probing function. CwA optimizes search performance directly for the query distribution. It minimizes its objective by alternating two steps: (i) gradient descent on the neural network of the probing function, and (ii) a large-scale combinatorial optimization of the cluster assignment for the database vectors. We solve the latter with a parallelizable auction algorithm that balances the partition by design. To further scale CwA, we extend the method to a Cartesian product of clusters that increases the partition's granularity. When database and query distributions differ, CwA achieves up to 4.7$\times$ throughput over the state-of-the-art at equal recall. In the in-distribution (ID) setting, even a simple linear probing function trained with CwA outperforms competing deep neural methods.

</details>


### [259] [Optimizing Visibility in Generative Engines: A Critical Survey of Generative Engine Optimization (2023-2026)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.14035)
*Olivier Martinez*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文对生成式引擎优化（GEO）领域进行了系统性批判性综述，指出GEO并非单一排序任务，而是一个包含搜索激活、爬取索引、检索重排、上下文分配、引用、显著性、事实吸收、保真度和用户行为的随机、部分可观测的管道。基于45项研究的分析表明，现有证据范围狭窄：已检索内容可以因果性地改变其引用或使用方式，但没有技术能稳定、长期、跨平台地影响有机可发现性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GEO领域自奠基性论文以来迅速扩张，但术语、指标和证据标准仍然异质，缺乏系统性的批判性梳理和评估。

Method: 对2023年11月至2026年7月期间的45项研究进行批判性综述，提出了多阶段形式化模型、可见性向量（区分可发现性、引用、吸收和经济结果）、证据层级，以及基于重复测量、释义、对照、人工验证和多智能体干扰的可重复实验协议。

Result: 奠基性论文报告的效果在其实验设定下有效，但前提是内容已存在于固定上下文中；既不能建立有机可发现性，也不能产生持久的流量效应。主题相关性和上下文位置是最可复现的杠杆，通用启发式方法迁移效果差，竞争会侵蚀个体收益，面向引用的改写可能损害检索。商业审计进一步揭示来源重叠度低、运行间变异性大、保真度差距持续存在。

Conclusion: 当前GEO的证据范围狭窄：已检索内容可以因果性地改变其引用或使用方式，但没有审查过的技术能展示出对有机可发现性或下游行为的稳定、纵向、跨平台因果效应。

Abstract: Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) seeks to increase content's presence, likelihood of citation, or influence in answers produced by generative engines. Since the foundational GEO paper, the field has expanded rapidly, but terminology, metrics, and evidence standards remain heterogeneous. This critical survey reviews 45 studies selected under a November 2023-July 2026 publication window, including one earlier preprint published at EMNLP after the window opened, plus relevant RAG and evaluation work. We argue that GEO is not a single ranking task but a stochastic, partially observable pipeline spanning search activation, crawling and indexing, retrieval, reranking and context allocation, citation, prominence, factual absorption, fidelity, and user behavior. The foundational paper's widely cited gains are valid within its experimental setting but conditional on a source already being present in a fixed context; they establish neither organic discoverability nor durable traffic effects. Reviewed work indicates that topical relevance and context position are the most reproducible levers, generic heuristics transfer poorly, competition can erode individual gains, and citation-oriented rewrites can impair retrieval. Commercial audits further reveal low source overlap, substantial run-to-run variability, and persistent fidelity gaps. We contribute a multistage formal model, a visibility vector separating discoverability, citation, absorption, and economic outcomes, an evidence hierarchy, and a reproducible protocol based on repeated measurements, paraphrases, controls, human validation, and multi-actor interference. Within this corpus, the evidence is narrow: already-retrieved content can causally alter its citation or use, but no reviewed technique shows a stable, longitudinal, cross-platform causal effect on organic discoverability or downstream behavior.

</details>

# eess.IV [[Back]](#toc)

### [260] [Prospective clinical indication, post-hoc report leakage, and fusion design in multi-image chest radiograph classification: a patient-clustered evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13800)
*Kamran Shahid,Muhammad Munwar Iqbal*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本研究评估了15,000个胸部X光片研究，比较了多种多模态融合方法。结果表明，临床指征与报告衍生的目标强相关，置换感知融合具有竞争力，而事后报告文本存在严重的报告-标签循环问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胸部X光片数据集中常混合图像、临床指征、发现和印象（Impression）等多源信息，但这些信息产生于不同的诊疗阶段，可能导致数据泄漏和循环性问题。作者旨在评估不同模态组合对模型性能的影响，特别是区分前瞻性（如临床指征）和事后（如发现、印象）信息的作用。

Method: 使用15,000个ReXGradient-160K研究（含两张可读图像和CheXbert衍生的五个报告观察标签）。采用冻结的DenseNet-121（图像）和Bio+ClinicalBERT（文本）编码器，比较了六种模型：仅图像、仅指征、固定顺序多模态、随机交换、DeepSets和SectionGuard-MI。使用五个种子训练，并通过2,000个患者聚类bootstrap估计不确定性。

Result: U-Ones指标下，宏AUROC：单张图像0.643，两张图像0.694，仅临床指征0.749，普通双图像+指征融合0.780。SectionGuard-MI达到AUROC 0.783和AUPRC 0.260。相较于普通融合，SectionGuard-MI的AUROC差异不显著（+0.0031, p=0.374），但AUPRC差异显著（+0.0289, p=0.004）。DeepSets获得最高AUROC点估计（0.787），随机交换融合获得最高AUPRC点估计（0.265）。完整报告文本达到了AUROC 0.979和AUPRC 0.836。

Conclusion: 前瞻性临床指征与报告衍生的目标标签之间存在强关联；置换感知的融合方法（如DeepSets、随机交换）具有竞争力；事后报告文本（发现、印象）会引入严重的报告-标签循环问题，导致性能虚高，应谨慎使用。

Abstract: Chest radiograph datasets often combine multiple images with Clinical Indication, Findings, and Impression, although these inputs are produced at different stages of care. We evaluated 15,000 ReXGradient-160K studies with two readable images and five CheXbert-derived report observations. Frozen DenseNet-121 and Bio+ClinicalBERT encoders were used to compare image-only, Indication-only, fixed-order multimodal, random-swap, DeepSets, and SectionGuard-MI models. Findings and Impression were evaluated only as post-hoc leakage controls. Models were trained with five seeds, and public-test uncertainty was estimated with 2,000 patient-cluster bootstrap replicates. Under U-Ones, macro AUROC was 0.643 for the primary image, 0.694 for two images, 0.749 for Indication, and 0.780 for ordinary two-image-plus-Indication fusion. SectionGuard-MI achieved AUROC 0.783 and AUPRC 0.260. Relative to ordinary fusion, its paired AUROC difference was 0.0031 (95% CI, -0.0042 to 0.0104; adjusted p=0.374), while its AUPRC difference was 0.0289 (95% CI, 0.0095 to 0.0413; adjusted p=0.004). DeepSets had the highest prospective AUROC point estimate (0.787), and random-swap fusion had the highest prospective AUPRC point estimate (0.265) with better calibration than SectionGuard-MI. Full report text alone reached AUROC 0.979 and AUPRC 0.836; AUROC remained above 0.973 after exact or expanded masking. These results show that prospective Indication is strongly associated with report-derived targets, permutation-aware fusion is competitive, and post-hoc report text creates substantial report-label circularity.

</details>

### [261] [A Better-than-$e^{1/e}$ Approximation Algorithm for Nash Social Welfare under Additive Valuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13340)
*Vignesh Viswanathan*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在加性估值下最大化纳什社会福利的近似算法，近似比为 e^{1/e} - c（c>0），优于此前 e^{1/e} 的最佳近似比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳什社会福利是公平分配中的重要目标函数，此前已知的最佳近似比为 e^{1/e}，作者希望突破这一界限，获得更优的近似算法。

Method: 本文通过某种技术手段（摘要未详述）构造了一个近似算法，实现了 e^{1/e} - c 的近似比，其中 c 为某个正常数。

Result: 得到了 e^{1/e} - c 的近似比，严格优于此前 e^{1/e} 的近似比。

Conclusion: 在加性估值下最大化纳什社会福利问题上取得了理论上的突破，改进了已有结果。

Abstract: We present an $(e^{1/e} - c)$-approximation algorithm for maximizing Nash social welfare under additive valuations, for some constant $c > 0$. This result improves upon the previous best-known approximation factor of $e^{1/e}$ [Barman, Krishnamurthy and Vaish, EC 2018].

</details>


### [262] [Auctions with Contract Design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13795)
*Xiaolin Bu,Jiarong Jin,Junzhu Ke,Pinyan Lu,Biaoshuai Tao,Xiang Yan,Chunxue Yang,Haikuo Yang,Zhihua Zhu*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究将质量合同融入拍卖的机制设计，证明在竞标者数量大时，拍卖方最优策略是将质量价值完全传递给获胜者，且该结论在不同拍卖规则下具有收入等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统拍卖中，竞标者的质量提升努力在分配前已成为沉没成本，导致道德风险问题（担心落标而抑制投资）。本文旨在设计一种将合同与拍卖结合的机制，通过事后质量奖励激励竞标者的前期投入。

Method: 建立拍卖理论+委托代理模型的统一框架，分别考察二价拍卖和一价拍卖。在对称贝叶斯纳什均衡假设下，研究线性合同，推导最大化拍卖方收入的最优奖励因子，并证明收入等价定理。

Result: 主要结果为：当竞标者数量趋近无穷时，最优奖励因子收敛于拍卖方从质量中获得的边际收益——即完全将质量价值传递给获胜者。该结论在二价与一价拍卖中均成立（收入等价）。相比无质量奖励的标准拍卖，合同机制能有效提升收入。

Conclusion: 本文证明在大规模竞标场景下，拍卖方应通过线性合同将质量的全部边际价值回馈给获胜者，以最大化自身收益。该设计原则具有跨拍卖规则的稳健性，且显著优于传统拍卖。

Abstract: We consider a new auction model where the bidders' utilities and the auctioneer's revenue depend on a quality factor of the transaction determined by costly and strategic investments of the bidders. Applications of our model include ad auctions, government concessions and crowdsourcing contests. Crucially, these quality-enhancing efforts made by the bidders are often sunk costs incurred prior to the allocation, creating a fundamental moral hazard problem where the risk of losing the auction discourages investments.
  In this paper, we study the design of revenue-maximizing contracts integrated into auctions: the auctioneer commits to a transfer rule that rewards the winner for the ex-post realized quality of the transaction to incentivize higher effort. Our new framework is a natural generalization of both the auction theory and the principal-agent model. We consider both the second-price and the first-price auctions. We show that natural symmetric Bayes Nash equilibria exist in both auctions. Assuming these natural equilibria are played by the bidders and the number of bidders is large, we study linear contracts and derive the optimal reward factor of the transfer rule that maximizes the auctioneer's revenue. As the main result, we show that the optimal reward factor converges to the auctioneer's marginal benefit from the quality, as the number of bidders grows. That is, it is optimal for the auctioneer to fully pass through the quality value to the winner. This observation is largely independent of the auction rule used: we derive a revenue equivalence theorem showing that the revenue remains the same as long as symmetric Bayes Nash equilibria exist. Lastly, by quantitatively comparing with the standard auctions where no quality reward is used, we show that the use of contracts effectively improves the revenue by incentivizing high investments from the bidders.

</details>


### [263] [Tighter Bounds for the Random-Offerer Mechanism in Bilateral Trade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.13959)
*Sunghyeon Jo*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究双边贸易中的随机出价机制（random-offerer mechanism），将其贸易收益与最优收益之比的下确界从约0.317844改进到1/π≈0.318310，并将上界从2.0749改进到约2.17277，从而将机制效率的精确范围压缩到[1/π, 0.46024)之间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双边贸易中，如何设计机制实现高效交易是核心问题。随机出价机制是简单且实用的机制，但其相对于最优（first-best）贸易收益的效率边界尚未精确确定，本文旨在进一步缩小该效率比率的已知范围。

Method: 下界证明采用参数化拉格朗日界方法，针对逐点单调的分配函数，在乘子为1时系数为2/π，拉格朗日项分解为卖方出价与买方出价两个独立利润项分别控制。上界通过构造具体分布族实现：买方为截断等收入分布，卖方为倾斜幂律下尾加常数虚拟成本段，并用严格区间算术验证数值不等式。

Result: 下界从约0.317844提升至1/π≈0.318310；上界构造出FB/RO > 2.17276852308451的实例，对应效率比率上界<0.460242308085529，改进了此前2.0749的比值。

Conclusion: 随机出价机制的效率比严格位于[1/π, 0.460242308085529)区间内，下界逼近1/π，上界通过构造更优的反例得到显著提升，为进一步确定精确常数提供了更紧的边界。

Abstract: The random-offerer mechanism for bilateral trade selects the seller or the buyer uniformly and lets the selected agent make a profit-maximizing take-it-or-leave-it offer. Let $ρ_{\rm RO}$ be the infimum, over independent value distributions, of the mechanism's gains from trade divided by first-best gains from trade. We prove $\frac1π\le ρ_{\rm RO}<0.460242308085529$.
  For the lower bound, we improve the previous guarantee from approximately $0.317844$ to $1/π\approx 0.318310$. The proof uses a parameterized Lagrangian bound for pointwise-monotone allocations. At multiplier one, this bound has coefficient $2/π$, and the Lagrangian separates into two terms controlled by the optimal seller-offering and buyer-offering profits. For the upper bound, we construct an explicit family consisting of a truncated equal-revenue buyer and a seller distribution with a tilted power-law lower tail and a constant-virtual-cost segment. The family satisfies $\operatorname{FB}/\operatorname{RO}>2.17276852308451$, improving the previous explicit ratio $2.0749$; rigorous interval arithmetic certifies the numerical inequality.

</details>
